function set_key_colors
	idx25{int} := 0
	idx25{int} := 0
	while(idx25{int} <= 127) 
		set_key_color(idx25{int}, KEY_COLOR_WHITE{int}){Builtin, None}
		if((idx25{int} >= 55) and (idx25{int} <= 96))
			set_key_color(idx25{int}, KEY_COLOR_BLUE{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(idx25{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function keyswitches_color_keys
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
		set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_RED{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 8) + i{int}]{int} {_keyswitch_states}  = ON{int})
			set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_ORANGE{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function articulations_compute_level
	subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} := 0
	i1200{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_start[(group_count0{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_id1{int} * 4) + _ret660{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations_start} 
	result1500{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[(group_count0{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_id1{int} * 4) + _ret660{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in} 
	_ret4000{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_end[(group_count0{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_id1{int} * 4) + _ret660{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations_end} 
	offset10{int} := _loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[(group_count0{int} * 32) + ((subarticulation_id1{int} * 4) + _ret660{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out} 
	if(in_range(modulation_positions[purge_state0{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} {modulation_positions} , i1200{int}, _ret4000{int}){Builtin, None})
		subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} := 1
		if(in_range(modulation_positions[purge_state0{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} {modulation_positions} , i1200{int}, i1200{int} + result1500{int}){Builtin, None} and (result1500{int} > 0))
			subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} := real(modulation_positions[purge_state0{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} {modulation_positions}  - i1200{int}){Builtin, None} / real(result1500{int}){Builtin, None}
		else
			if(in_range(modulation_positions[purge_state0{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} {modulation_positions} , _ret4000{int} - offset10{int}, _ret4000{int}){Builtin, None} and (offset10{int} > 0))
				subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} := real(_ret4000{int} - modulation_positions[purge_state0{int} * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} {modulation_positions} ){Builtin, None} / real(offset10{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if

function last_transitions_update
	i11000{int} := 0
	i11000{int} := 0
	while(i11000{int} <= (num_elements(_last_transitions{int[]} {_last_transitions} ){Builtin, None} - 1)) 
		if(_last_transitions[i11000{int}]{int} {_last_transitions}  # - 1)
			if(_last_transitions_timecode[i11000{int}]{int} {_last_transitions_timecode}  < (ENGINE_UPTIME{int} - 2000))
				_last_transitions[i11000{int}]{int} {_last_transitions}  := - 1
			end if
		end if
		inc(i11000{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

end function

function repetition_engine_update_tempo
	subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} / 960
	if((subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} # tempo{real}) or (NI_CALLBACK_TYPE{int} # NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER{int}))
		rr10{int} := 0
		fade_in_start01{int} := 0
		fade_in_range01{int} := 0
		rr10{int} := 0
		while(rr10{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
			fade_in_start01{int} := 0
			while(fade_in_start01{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
				fade_in_range01{int} := 0
				while(fade_in_range01{int} <= (NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS{int} - 1)) 
					if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(rr10{int} * 32) + ((fade_in_start01{int} * 4) + fade_in_range01{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type}  = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_REPETITION{int})
						_repetition_interval_time[(rr10{int} * 4096) + ((fade_in_start01{int} * 512) + fade_in_range01{int})]{int} {_repetition_interval_time}  := int((60000 / subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real}) * (4 / real(_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[(rr10{int} * 32) + ((fade_in_start01{int} * 4) + fade_in_range01{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed} ){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}
					end if
					inc(fade_in_range01{int}){Builtin, None}
				end while
				inc(fade_in_start01{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
			inc(rr10{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		tempo{real} := subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real}
	end if
end function

	if(repetition_engine_active{int} = TRUE{int})

function find_loaded_legato
	authoring_page_active{int} := FALSE{int}
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  # - 1)
		if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type}  = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{int})
			authoring_page_active{int} := TRUE{int}
			set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_authoring_legato_title{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{string} {subarticulations_full_name}  & " (" & _loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  & ")"){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function authoring_open
	call find_loaded_legato{UserDefined, Call}
	idx25{int} := 60
	subarticulation_event1{int} := 60
	iii1{int} := 0
	call update_authoring_transition{UserDefined, Call}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_authoring{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_subarticulation_selection
	group_count001{int} := selected_subarticulation{int}
	group_count000{int} := subarticulation_event1{int}
	idx25{int} := 0
	idx25{int} := 0
	while(idx25{int} <= (num_elements(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection{int[]} {btn_edit_subarticulation_selection} ){Builtin, None} - 1)) 
		if(idx25{int} # group_count001{int})
			set_control_par(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[idx25{int}]{int} {btn_edit_subarticulation_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
		else
			set_control_par(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[idx25{int}]{int} {btn_edit_subarticulation_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, ON{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(idx25{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  # - 1)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_subarticulation_title{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, "    " & subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{string} {subarticulations_full_name} ){Builtin, None}

		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_subarticulation_title{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, "    Empty"){Builtin, None}

	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_solo_subarticulation{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, _subarticulations_solo_states[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} {_subarticulations_solo_states} ){Builtin, None}

function subarticulation_browser_open
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_subarticulation_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  # - 1)
		idx25{int} := type_to_category[subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type} ]{int} {type_to_category} 
		subarticulation_event1{int} := idx25{int}
		idx25{int} := 0
		idx25{int} := 0
		while(idx25{int} <= (num_elements(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection{int[]} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} ){Builtin, None} - 1)) 
			set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[idx25{int}]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
			if(_subarticulation_browser_entries[(idx25{int} * 14) + idx25{int}]{int} {_subarticulation_browser_entries}  # - 1)
				set_control_par_str(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[idx25{int}]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_subarticulation_browser_entries[(idx25{int} * 14) + idx25{int}]{int} {_subarticulation_browser_entries} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{string} {subarticulations_full_name} ){Builtin, None}
				if(_subarticulation_browser_entries[(idx25{int} * 14) + idx25{int}]{int} {_subarticulation_browser_entries}  = _loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} )
					set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[idx25{int}]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, ON{int}){Builtin, None}
				else
					set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[idx25{int}]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
				end if
				set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[idx25{int}]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_selection} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			inc(idx25{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		idx25{int} := 0
		while(idx25{int} <= (num_elements(btn_subarticulation_browser_category{int[]} {btn_subarticulation_browser_category} ){Builtin, None} - 1)) 
			if(idx25{int} = idx25{int})
				set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_category[idx25{int}]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_category} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, ON{int}){Builtin, None}
			else
				set_control_par(btn_subarticulation_browser_category[idx25{int}]{int} {btn_subarticulation_browser_category} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, OFF{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			inc(idx25{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		subarticulation_browser_active_category{int} := idx25{int}
	end if
end function

end function

function update_modwheel_assignment_circles
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_left} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_right} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(_loaded_subarticulations[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  # - 1)
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_left} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_right} , CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			if(i{int} = selected_subarticulation{int})
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle} , CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_left} , CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_right} , CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			else
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle} , CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_left} , CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_right} , CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_left} , CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, _loaded_subarticulations_start[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations_start} ){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int} {lbl_center_circle_bound_right} , CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, 127 - _loaded_subarticulations_end[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + i{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations_end} ){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update_dynamic_range_control

	xy_dynamic_range[2]{real} {xy_dynamic_range}  := real(_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[(selected_instrument{int} * 32) + ((selected_keyswitch{int} * 4) + selected_subarticulation{int})]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper} ){Builtin, None} / 127
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_dynamic_range[0]{real} {xy_dynamic_range}  * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_dynamic_range[2]{real} {xy_dynamic_range}  * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_line{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	group_count001{int} := modulation_positions[0 * use_polyphonic_modulation{int}]{int} {modulation_positions} 
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_cursor{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, (get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - 5) + int((real(((group_count001{int} * (1 + (sh_right(127 - group_count001{int}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(group_count001{int} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}))) - (1 * sh_right(group_count001{int} - 1, 31){Builtin, None})) - (127 * sh_right(127 - group_count001{int}, 31){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None} / 127) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
end function

function center_circle_distance
	dx0{real} := transition_speed0{real} - 0.5
	dy0{real} := y3{real} - 0.5
	subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} := sqrt((dx0{real} * dx0{real}) + (dy0{real} * dy0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

function center_circle_angle
	dx0{real} := subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} - 0.5
	y3{real} := dy0{real} - 0.5
	cos_theta0{real} := dx0{real} / sqrt((dx0{real} * dx0{real}) + (y3{real} * y3{real})){Builtin, None}
	angle1{real} := acos(cos_theta0{real}){Builtin, None}
	if(y3{real} < 0)
		angle1{real} := (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real}) - angle1{real}
	end if
	transition_speed0{real} := angle1{real}
end function

function angle_to_value
	subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} := y3{real} + (NI_MATH_PI{real} / 2)
	if(subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} > (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2))
		subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} := subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})
	end if
	subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} := abs(subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})){Builtin, None}
	group_count001{int} := int((127 * (subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} - dx0{real})) / (dy0{real} - dx0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

function move_to_legato_buffer

	i1200{int} := 0
	result1500{int} := 0
	result150{int} := 0
	while(result150{int} <= (MAX_TRANSITION_DYN_LAYERS{int} - 1)) 
		i1200{int} := 0
		while(i1200{int} <= 127) 
			result1500{int} := 0
			while(result1500{int} <= (MAX_TRANSITIONS_PER_NOTE{int} - 1)) 
				_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[(result150{int} * 3200) + ((i1200{int} * 25) + result1500{int})]{int} {_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time}  := _legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[(group_count000{int} * 204800) + ((string02{int} * 25600) + ((ii4{int} * 6400) + ((result150{int} * 3200) + ((i1200{int} * 25) + result1500{int}))))]{int} {_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time}
